  <script type="text/javascript">
   jQuery(document).ready(function() {
				// CUSTOM AJAX CONTENT LOADING FUNCTION
				var ajaxRevslider = function(obj) {
				
					// obj.type : Post Type
					// obj.id : ID of Content to Load
					// obj.aspectratio : The Aspect Ratio of the Container / Media
					// obj.selector : The Container Selector where the Content of Ajax will be injected. It is done via the Essential Grid on Return of Content
					
					var content = "";

					data = {};
					
					data.action = 'revslider_ajax_call_front';
					data.client_action = 'get_slider_html';
					data.token = '46bae8ae6d';
					data.type = obj.type;
					data.id = obj.id;
					data.aspectratio = obj.aspectratio;
					
					// SYNC AJAX REQUEST
					jQuery.ajax({
						type:"post",
						url:"http://www.capturebilling.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php",
						dataType: 'json',
						data:data,
						async:false,
						success: function(ret, textStatus, XMLHttpRequest) {
							if(ret.success == true)
								content = ret.data;								
						},
						error: function(e) {
							console.log(e);
						}
					});
					
					 // FIRST RETURN THE CONTENT WHEN IT IS LOADED !!
					 return content;						 
				};
				
				// CUSTOM AJAX FUNCTION TO REMOVE THE SLIDER
				var ajaxRemoveRevslider = function(obj) {
					return jQuery(obj.selector+" .rev_slider").revkill();
				};

				// EXTEND THE AJAX CONTENT LOADING TYPES WITH TYPE AND FUNCTION
				var extendessential = setInterval(function() {
					if (jQuery.fn.tpessential != undefined) {
						clearInterval(extendessential);
						if(typeof(jQuery.fn.tpessential.defaults) !== 'undefined') {
							jQuery.fn.tpessential.defaults.ajaxTypes.push({type:"revslider",func:ajaxRevslider,killfunc:ajaxRemoveRevslider,openAnimationSpeed:0.3});   
							// type:  Name of the Post to load via Ajax into the Essential Grid Ajax Container
							// func: the Function Name which is Called once the Item with the Post Type has been clicked
							// killfunc: function to kill in case the Ajax Window going to be removed (before Remove function !
							// openAnimationSpeed: how quick the Ajax Content window should be animated (default is 0.3)
						}
					}
				},30);
			});
  </script>

            <h2>
             Nursing is Rough so Take a Break and Read a Nurse Blog
            </h2>
            <p>
             Life as a nurse could provide the most rewarding moments. But with hectic, sometimes unpredictable, 24-hour shifts, it is also considered one of the mostdemanding medical professions today.
             <span id="more-6589">
             </span>
            </p>
            <p>
             With this in mind myfriends at
             <a href="http://www.soliant.com/nursing/travel-nursing-jobs/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.soliant.com/nursing/travel-nursing-jobs/', 'Soliant Health');" rel="nofollow">
              Soliant Health
             </a>
             have put together an infographic to serve as a resource of sorts for nurses everywhere. Theyve highlighted those in the nurse blogosphere who offered the most helpful information, up-to-date news and entertaining stories. Each nurse blog offers a unique, and at times humorous perspective into the day-to-day lives of nursing professionals.
            </p>
            <p>
             The responsibilities of nurses will only continue to mount with time, but there are a number of resources out there to give you that much needed supportwhether its in the form of a belly-aching laugh or even just a simple smile. Your much needed escape is only a mouse-click away!
            </p>
            <p style="text-align: center;">
             <a href="http://www.capturebilling.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/03/Soliant-Nurses-Online-For-Nurses-Offline.png">
              <img alt="Infographic: Soliant Nurses Online for Nurses Offline" class=" wp-image-6590 aligncenter" height="3269" src="http://www.capturebilling.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/03/Soliant-Nurses-Online-For-Nurses-Offline.png" title="Infographic: Soliant Nurses Online for Nurses Offline" width="540"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p style="text-align: center;">
             This infographic is from Soliant Health at the URL:
             <br/>
             <a href="http://www.soliant.com/nursing/travel-nursing-jobs/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.soliant.com/nursing/travel-nursing-jobs/', 'http://www.soliant.com/nursing/travel-nursing-jobs/');" rel="nofollow">
              http://www.soliant.com/nursing/travel-nursing-jobs/
             </a>
            </p>
            <h3 style="text-align: center;">
             Here is the list of Nursing Blogs mentioned above.
            </h3>
            <p style="text-align: center;">
             <a href="http://crasspollination.blogspot.com/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://crasspollination.blogspot.com/', 'crasspollination.blogspot.com');" rel="nofollow">
              crasspollination.blogspot.com
             </a>
             <br/>
             <a href="http://newnurseinthehood.blogspot.com/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://newnurseinthehood.blogspot.com/', 'newnurseinthehood.blogspot.com');" rel="nofollow">
              newnurseinthehood.blogspot.com
             </a>
             <br/>
             <a href="http://www.impactednurse.com/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.impactednurse.com/', 'impactednurse.com');" rel="nofollow">
              impactednurse.com
             </a>
             <br/>
             <a href="http://nursexy.blogspot.com/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://nursexy.blogspot.com/', 'nursexy.blogspot.com');" rel="nofollow">
              nursexy.blogspot.com
             </a>
             <br/>
             <a href="http://www.codeblog.com/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.codeblog.com/', 'codeblog.com');" rel="nofollow">
              codeblog.com
             </a>
             <br/>
             <a href="http://www.thenerdynurse.com/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.thenerdynurse.com/', 'thenerdynurse.com');" rel="nofollow">
              thenerdynurse.com
             </a>
             <br/>
             <a href="http://www.childrenarepresent.com/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.childrenarepresent.com/', 'childrenarepresent.com');" rel="nofollow">
              childrenarepresent.com
             </a>
             <br/>
             <a href="http://atyourcervix.blogspot.com/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://atyourcervix.blogspot.com/', 'atyourcervix.blogspot.com');" rel="nofollow">
              atyourcervix.blogspot.com
             </a>
             <br/>
             <a href="http://whatwecallnursing.tumblr.com/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://whatwecallnursing.tumblr.com/', 'whatwecallnursing.tumblr.com');" rel="nofollow">
              whatwecallnursing.tumblr.com
             </a>
             <br/>
             <a href="http://whatshouldwecallnursingschool.tumblr.com/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://whatshouldwecallnursingschool.tumblr.com/', 'whatshouldwecallnursingschool.tumblr.com');" rel="nofollow">
              whatshouldwecallnursingschool.tumblr.com
             </a>
             <br/>
             <a href="http://nurseconfessions.tumblr.com/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://nurseconfessions.tumblr.com/', 'nurseconfessions.tumblr.com');" rel="nofollow">
              nurseconfessions.tumblr.com
             </a>
             <br/>
             <a href="http://theartof-nursing.tumblr.com/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://theartof-nursing.tumblr.com/', 'theartof-nursing.tumblr.com');" rel="nofollow">
              theartof-nursing.tumblr.com
             </a>
            </p>
            <p style="text-align: left;">
             <span style="color: #800000; font-size: large;">
              <a href="http://clicktotweet.com/J16uO" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://clicktotweet.com/J16uO', '');" rel="nofollow">
               <img alt="Tweet to your Friends" class="alignright wp-image-6663" height="164" src="http://www.capturebilling.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/03/Tweet-This-Post.png" style="border: 0px;" width="168"/>
              </a>
              If you are a nurse have you visited any of these websites? If so tell us your favorites and why. Leave us a comment below.
             </span>
             <br/>
             <img alt="Arrow to Comments" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-6593" height="128" src="http://www.capturebilling.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/03/1362629379_emblem-downloads.png" style="border: 0px;" title="Arrow to Comments" width="128"/>
            </p>

       <div class="block block-type-text block-fluid-height block-mirrored block-mirroring-b4453ac93b9b6725 block-original-b4453bc4fe092803" data-alias="" id="block-b4453ac93b9b6725">
        <div class="block-content">
         <h1 class="block-title">
          <span>
           Disclaimer
          </span>
         </h1>
         <div class="entry-content">
          <p>
           The analysis of any medical billing or coding question is dependent on numerous specific facts -- including the factual situations present related to the patients, the practice, the professionals and the medical services and advice. Additionally, laws and regulations and insurance and payer policies (as well as coding itself) are subject to change. The information that has been accurate previously can be particularly dependent on changes in time or circumstances. The information contained in this web site is intended as general information only. It is not intended to serve as medical, health, legal or financial advice or as a substitute for professional advice of a medical coding professional, healthcare consultant, physician or medical professional, legal counsel, accountant or financial advisor. If you have a question about a specific matter, you should contact a professional advisor directly.
          </p>
         </div>
